          --mr-toggled-font-family: Monospace;
        }
        .container-issue {
          width: 100%;
          flex-direction: column;

        }

Email display settings

<h2>Email display settings</h2>



        

There is a 

setting

<a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a>

 to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.

<p>There is a <a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a> to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.</p>



        

Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.

<p>Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.</p>



        

If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to 

get
        involved

<a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a>

 in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.

<p>If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to <a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a> in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.</p>

This site hosts public issues in public projects

<h2>This site hosts public issues in public projects</h2>



        

Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.

<p>Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>



        

Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.

<p>Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.</p>

        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>

Date: Thu Jul 07 23:33:18 2022



<span class="line"><!---->Date: Thu Jul 07 23:33:18 2022<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Turn a SECURITY_DCHECK in |LayoutTableRow::AddChild| to CHECK



<span class="line"><!---->Turn a SECURITY_DCHECK in |LayoutTableRow::AddChild| to CHECK<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





When the |child| of the |LayoutTableRow::AddChild| is a



<span class="line"><!---->When the |child| of the |LayoutTableRow::AddChild| is a<!----></span>



<br>





|LayoutNGTableCell|, |child->IsTableCell()| is |true|, but



<span class="line"><!---->|LayoutNGTableCell|, |child-&gt;IsTableCell()| is |true|, but<!----></span>



<br>





|To<LayoutTableCell>(child)| causes a SECURITY_DCHECK. This



<span class="line"><!---->|To&lt;LayoutTableCell&gt;(child)| causes a SECURITY_DCHECK. This<!----></span>



<br>





patch turns it to a normal crash.



<span class="line"><!---->patch turns it to a normal crash.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





This happens when:



<span class="line"><!---->This happens when:<!----></span>



<br>





1. CSS Container Query 



<span class="line"><!---->1. CSS Container Query <!----></span>





crbug.com/1145970



<a class="strike-through" target="_blank" href="/p/chromium/issues/detail?id=1145970" title="Container Queries"><!---->crbug.com/1145970<!----></a>





 is enabled.



<span class="line"><!----> is enabled.<!----></span>



<br>





2. A table cell is added to a multi-column container, which



<span class="line"><!---->2. A table cell is added to a multi-column container, which<!----></span>



<br>





   creates a legacy anonymous table.



<span class="line"><!---->   creates a legacy anonymous table.<!----></span>



<br>





3. Then turn off the multi-column, causing reattach.



<span class="line"><!---->3. Then turn off the multi-column, causing reattach.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





When the CSS Container Query is enabled, the table cell will



<span class="line"><!---->When the CSS Container Query is enabled, the table cell will<!----></span>



<br>





be |LayoutNGTableCell|, but the legacy anonymous table is not



<span class="line"><!---->be |LayoutNGTableCell|, but the legacy anonymous table is not<!----></span>



<br>





removed. |LayoutObject::AddChild| tries to add the



<span class="line"><!---->removed. |LayoutObject::AddChild| tries to add the<!----></span>



<br>





|LayoutNGTableCell| to the legacy anonymous table, resulting



<span class="line"><!---->|LayoutNGTableCell| to the legacy anonymous table, resulting<!----></span>



<br>





this failure.



<span class="line"><!---->this failure.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>

SECURITY_DCHECK does not crash the browser on users machines, unfortunately. So proceeding past one tends to be a security vulnerability (not entirely unlike other DCHECKs)



<span class="line"><!---->SECURITY_DCHECK does not crash the browser on users machines, unfortunately. So proceeding past one tends to be a security vulnerability (not entirely unlike other DCHECKs)<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/main:third_party/blink/renderer/platform/wtf/assertions.h;l=46-67?ss=chromium%2Fchromium%2Fsrc&q=SECURITY_DCHECK



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/main:third_party/blink/renderer/platform/wtf/assertions.h;l=46-67?ss=chromium%2Fchromium%2Fsrc&amp;q=SECURITY_DCHECK"><!---->https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/main:third_party/blink/renderer/platform/wtf/assertions.h;l=46-67?ss=chromium%2Fchromium%2Fsrc&amp;q=SECURITY_DCHECK<!----></a>

<span class="line"><!---->*** Boilerplate reminders! ***<!----></span>



<br>





Please do NOT publicly disclose details until a fix has been released to all our users. Early public disclosure may cancel the provisional reward. Also, please be considerate about disclosure when the bug affects a core library that may be used by other products. Please do NOT share this information with third parties who are not directly involved in fixing the bug. Doing so may cancel the provisional reward. Please be honest if you have already disclosed anything publicly or to third parties. Lastly, we understand that some of you are not interested in money. We offer the option to donate your reward to an eligible charity. If you prefer this option, let us know and we will also match your donation - subject to our discretion. Any rewards that are unclaimed after 12 months will be donated to a charity of our choosing.
